</span><span id="L-288"><a href="#L-288"><span class="linenos"> 288</span></a>    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="fm">__mul__</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">other</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Union</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nb">float</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nb">int</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s1">&#39;CoordinateVectorNd&#39;</span><span class="p">])</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="s1">&#39;CoordinateVectorNd&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="L-289"><a href="#L-289"><span class="linenos"> 289</span></a><span class="w">        </span><span class="sd">&quot;&quot;&quot;Multiplication to number or to other coordinate vector (item by item)</span>
</span><span id="L-290"><a href="#L-290"><span class="linenos"> 290</span></a>
</span><span id="L-291"><a href="#L-291"><span class="linenos"> 291</span></a><span class="sd">        v1 = [1, 2, 3]</span>
</span><span id="L-292"><a href="#L-292"><span class="linenos"> 292</span></a><span class="sd">        v2 = [2, 3, 1]</span>
</span><span id="L-293"><a href="#L-293"><span class="linenos"> 293</span></a><span class="sd">        v3 = v1 * v2 = [1 * 2, 2 * 3, 3 * 1] = [2, 6, 3]</span>
</span><span id="L-294"><a href="#L-294"><span class="linenos"> 294</span></a>
</span><span id="L-295"><a href="#L-295"><span class="linenos"> 295</span></a><span class="sd">        Args:</span>

</span><span id="L-877"><a href="#L-877"><span class="linenos"> 877</span></a>    <span class="c1"># TODO: Другие операции умножения применимые к координатным векторам - реализовать в методах.</span>
</span><span id="L-878"><a href="#L-878"><span class="linenos"> 878</span></a>    <span class="c1"># А неприменимые - в соответствующих классах (например DirectedGraphNd отлично подходит на роль </span>

        <span class="name">copy</span><span class="signature pdoc-code condensed">(<span class="param"><span class="bp">self</span></span><span class="return-annotation">) -> <span class="n"><a href="#VectorBase">VectorBase</a></span>:</span></span>

                <label class="view-source-button" for="VectorBase.copy-view-source"><span>View Source</span></label>

    </div>
    <a class="headerlink" href="#VectorBase.copy"></a>
            <div class="pdoc-code codehilite"><pre><span></span><span id="VectorBase.copy-57"><a href="#VectorBase.copy-57"><span class="linenos">57</span></a>    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">copy</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="s1">&#39;VectorBase&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="VectorBase.copy-58"><a href="#VectorBase.copy-58"><span class="linenos">58</span></a>        <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="ne">NotImplementedError</span>
</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Should make relevant copy of an object (not so general and deep as a deepcopy()). should copy only known object fields.
Example:
    def copy(self):
        cls = self.__class__
        result = cls.__new__(cls)
        result.__dict__['dimension'] = self.dimension
        result.__dict__['_point'] = self._point.copy()
        return result</p>

<p>Raises:
    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
</div>


                            </div>
                            <div id="VectorBase.shallow_copy" class="classattr">
                                        <input id="VectorBase.shallow_copy-view-source" class="view-source-toggle-state" type="checkbox" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1">
<div class="attr function">
            
        <span class="def">def</span>
        <span class="name">shallow_copy</span><span class="signature pdoc-code condensed">(<span class="param"><span class="bp">self</span></span><span class="return-annotation">) -> <span class="n"><a href="#VectorBase">VectorBase</a></span>:</span></span>

                <label class="view-source-button" for="VectorBase.shallow_copy-view-source"><span>View Source</span></label>

    </div>
    <a class="headerlink" href="#VectorBase.shallow_copy"></a>
            <div class="pdoc-code codehilite"><pre><span></span><span id="VectorBase.shallow_copy-60"><a href="#VectorBase.shallow_copy-60"><span class="linenos">60</span></a>    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">shallow_copy</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="s1">&#39;VectorBase&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="VectorBase.shallow_copy-61"><a href="#VectorBase.shallow_copy-61"><span class="linenos">61</span></a>        <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="ne">NotImplementedError</span>
</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Same as copy.copy(self), but should copy only known object fields.
Example:
    def shallow_copy(self):
        cls = self.__class__
        result = cls.__new__(cls)
        result.__dict__['dimension'] = self.dimension
        result.__dict__['_point'] = self._point
        return result</p>

<p>Raises:
    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
</div>


                            </div>
                            <div id="VectorBase.updated_copy" class="classattr">
                                        <input id="VectorBase.updated_copy-view-source" class="view-source-toggle-state" type="checkbox" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1">
<div class="attr function">
            
        <span class="def">def</span>
        <span class="name">updated_copy</span><span class="signature pdoc-code multiline">(<span class="param">	<span class="bp">self</span>,</span><span class="param">	<span class="n">update</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Dict</span></span><span class="return-annotation">) -> <span class="n"><a href="#VectorBase">VectorBase</a></span>:</span></span>

                <label class="view-source-button" for="VectorBase.updated_copy-view-source"><span>View Source</span></label>

    </div>
    <a class="headerlink" href="#VectorBase.updated_copy"></a>
            <div class="pdoc-code codehilite"><pre><span></span><span id="VectorBase.updated_copy-63"><a href="#VectorBase.updated_copy-63"><span class="linenos">63</span></a>    <span class="k">def</span> <span class="nf">updated_copy</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">self</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="n">update</span><span class="p">:</span> <span class="n">Dict</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="o">-&gt;</span> <span class="s1">&#39;VectorBase&#39;</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="VectorBase.updated_copy-64"><a href="#VectorBase.updated_copy-64"><span class="linenos">64</span></a>        <span class="k">raise</span> <span class="ne">NotImplementedError</span>
</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Will make updated copy of an object. Other behavior should be the same as in the <code>def copy(self)</code> method.
Example:
    # from cengal.data_manipulation.get_dict_key_with_callable_default import get_dict_key_with_callable_default
    from cengal.entities.copyable import CopyableMixin, get_dict_key_with_callable_default</p>

<pre><code>def updated_copy(self, update: Dict):
    cls = self.__class__
    result = cls.__new__(cls)
    result.__dict__['dimension'] = update.get('dimension', self.dimension)
    result.__dict__['_point'] = get_dict_key_with_callable_default(update, '_point', lambda: self._point.copy())
    return result
</code></pre>

<p>Raises:
    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
</div>

            <div class="docstring"><p>Should make relevant copy of an object (not so general and deep as a deepcopy()). should copy only known object fields.
Example:
    def copy(self):
        cls = self.__class__
        result = cls.__new__(cls)
        result.__dict__['dimension'] = self.dimension
        result.__dict__['_point'] = self._point.copy()
        return result</p>

    def shallow_copy(self):
        cls = self.__class__

</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Will make updated copy of an object. Other behavior should be the same as in the <code>def copy(self)</code> method.
Example:
    # from cengal.data_manipulation.get_dict_key_with_callable_default import get_dict_key_with_callable_default
    from cengal.entities.copyable import CopyableMixin, get_dict_key_with_callable_default</p>

<pre><code>def updated_copy(self, update: Dict):
    cls = self.__class__
    result = cls.__new__(cls)
    result.__dict__['dimension'] = update.get('dimension', self.dimension)
    result.__dict__['_point'] = get_dict_key_with_callable_default(update, '_point', lambda: self._point.copy())
    return result
</code></pre>

<p>Raises:
    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
</div>

</span><span id="VectorNd.copy-900"><a href="#VectorNd.copy-900"><span class="linenos">900</span></a>        <span class="n">result</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="vm">__dict__</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;terminal_point&#39;</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">terminal_point</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">copy</span><span class="p">()</span>
</span><span id="VectorNd.copy-901"><a href="#VectorNd.copy-901"><span class="linenos">901</span></a>        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">result</span>
</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Should make relevant copy of an object (not so general and deep as a deepcopy()). should copy only known object fields.
Example:
    def copy(self):
        cls = self.__class__
        result = cls.__new__(cls)
        result.__dict__['dimension'] = self.dimension
        result.__dict__['_point'] = self._point.copy()
        return result</p>

<p>Raises:
    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
</div>

</span><span id="VectorNd.shallow_copy-905"><a href="#VectorNd.shallow_copy-905"><span class="linenos">905</span></a>        <span class="n">result</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">cls</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="fm">__new__</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="bp">cls</span><span class="p">)</span>
</span><span id="VectorNd.shallow_copy-906"><a href="#VectorNd.shallow_copy-906"><span class="linenos">906</span></a>        <span class="n">result</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="vm">__dict__</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;initial_point&#39;</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">initial_point</span>
</span><span id="VectorNd.shallow_copy-907"><a href="#VectorNd.shallow_copy-907"><span class="linenos">907</span></a>        <span class="n">result</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="vm">__dict__</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;terminal_point&#39;</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">terminal_point</span>
</span><span id="VectorNd.shallow_copy-908"><a href="#VectorNd.shallow_copy-908"><span class="linenos">908</span></a>        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">result</span>
</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Same as copy.copy(self), but should copy only known object fields.
Example:
    def shallow_copy(self):
        cls = self.__class__
        result = cls.__new__(cls)
        result.__dict__['dimension'] = self.dimension
        result.__dict__['_point'] = self._point
        return result</p>

<p>Raises:
    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
</div>

</span><span id="VectorNd.updated_copy-915"><a href="#VectorNd.updated_copy-915"><span class="linenos">915</span></a>        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">result</span>
</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Will make updated copy of an object. Other behavior should be the same as in the <code>def copy(self)</code> method.
Example:
    # from cengal.data_manipulation.get_dict_key_with_callable_default import get_dict_key_with_callable_default
    from cengal.entities.copyable import CopyableMixin, get_dict_key_with_callable_default</p>

<pre><code>def updated_copy(self, update: Dict):
    cls = self.__class__
    result = cls.__new__(cls)
    result.__dict__['dimension'] = update.get('dimension', self.dimension)
    result.__dict__['_point'] = get_dict_key_with_callable_default(update, '_point', lambda: self._point.copy())
    return result
</code></pre>

<p>Raises:
    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
</div>

</span><span id="DirectedGraphNd.copy-1103"><a href="#DirectedGraphNd.copy-1103"><span class="linenos">1103</span></a>        <span class="k">if</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">points_list</span> <span class="ow">is</span> <span class="kc">None</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="DirectedGraphNd.copy-1104"><a href="#DirectedGraphNd.copy-1104"><span class="linenos">1104</span></a>            <span class="n">result</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="vm">__dict__</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;points_list&#39;</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">points_list</span>
</span><span id="DirectedGraphNd.copy-1105"><a href="#DirectedGraphNd.copy-1105"><span class="linenos">1105</span></a>        <span class="k">else</span><span class="p">:</span>
</span><span id="DirectedGraphNd.copy-1106"><a href="#DirectedGraphNd.copy-1106"><span class="linenos">1106</span></a>            <span class="n">result</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="vm">__dict__</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s1">&#39;points_list&#39;</span><span class="p">]</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="p">[</span><span class="n">point</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">copy</span><span class="p">()</span> <span class="k">for</span> <span class="n">point</span> <span class="ow">in</span> <span class="bp">self</span><span class="o">.</span><span class="n">points_list</span><span class="p">]</span>
</span><span id="DirectedGraphNd.copy-1107"><a href="#DirectedGraphNd.copy-1107"><span class="linenos">1107</span></a>
</span><span id="DirectedGraphNd.copy-1108"><a href="#DirectedGraphNd.copy-1108"><span class="linenos">1108</span></a>        <span class="k">return</span> <span class="n">result</span>
</span></pre></div>


            <div class="docstring"><p>Should make relevant copy of an object (not so general and deep as a deepcopy()). should copy only known object fields.
Example:
    def copy(self):
        cls = self.__class__
        result = cls.__new__(cls)
        result.__dict__['dimension'] = self.dimension
        result.__dict__['_point'] = self._point.copy()
        return result</p>

<p>Raises:
    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
</div>

    def shallow_copy(self):
        cls = self.__class__
        result = cls.__new__(cls)
        result.__dict__['dimension'] = self.dimension

        return result</p>

            <div class="docstring"><p>Will make updated copy of an object. Other behavior should be the same as in the <code>def copy(self)</code> method.
Example:
    # from cengal.data_manipulation.get_dict_key_with_callable_default import get_dict_key_with_callable_default
    from cengal.entities.copyable import CopyableMixin, get_dict_key_with_callable_default</p>

<pre><code>def updated_copy(self, update: Dict):
    cls = self.__class__
    result = cls.__new__(cls)
    result.__dict__['dimension'] = update.get('dimension', self.dimension)
    result.__dict__['_point'] = get_dict_key_with_callable_default(update, '_point', lambda: self._point.copy())
    return result
</code></pre>

    NotImplementedError: _description_</p>
